Galactic Trader: The Venom Blockchain Adventure

The game takes place in 8 galaxies from the computer game Elite of the 80s. Each galaxy has 255 NFT planets. Each planet has its own marketplace for resources that are mined on that planet.

At the beginning of the game, the player receives the smallest and simplest spaceship, with which he can buy goods on one planet and sell them on another. By earning income from arbitrage, the player can buy weapons and upgrades for his spaceship.

During the flight, the player can encounter pirates or hostile other players. In case of a meeting, a battle takes place, in which the winner can collect the cargo of the loser if he has free space in the hold.

The entire game takes place on the Venom blockchain, which ensures transparency and security of transactions, as well as protection against fraud. Each spaceship and each resource has its own unique NFT token, which can be bought, sold, or exchanged for other tokens. Players can earn real money by selling their tokens on a cryptocurrency exchange.

The game on the Venom blockchain is a unique experience that allows players to immerse themselves in an exciting space world and earn real money by playing an engaging game.

TVM Challenge for all smart contract developers with a prize pool of 30,000 TON!

Join our exciting contest and explore the new features and opcode usage cases introduced in the upcoming TVM update. This is your chance to showcase your skills and discover innovative possibilities for creating cutting-edge products on TON.

The best utilization of the new TVM features will be rewarded by our esteemed jury panel. Each project will be evaluated based on a set of criteria including relevance, efficiency, uniqueness of the idea, and technical difficulty. More details one may find in TON Blog.

The contest will run for 3 weeks, from June 2nd to June 25th, 2023. Submissions will be open starting June 18th in @toncontests_bot. You will need to provide the name of the project, short description, link to GitHub or project web-page and your TON wallet address.

To participate and dive deep into the resources to grasp the changes introduced in the upcoming TVM update:

üíé List of all new opcodes from the upcoming TVM update
üíé Git source code with the new TVM update
üíé Official TON Docs
üíé Blueprint/Sandbox with upgraded TVM support

Unleash your creativity and push the boundaries of smart contract development on TON. Good luck!

GOSH Announcements 06.06.2023 22:48:08
In reply to this message
üå≤GOSH is excited to announce the launch of AnyTree, the first software deployment system secured by a blockchain üå≤

AnyTree secures software at the source, with cryptographic signatures and Deep SBOM technology, pioneered by GOSH. This means that you can be confident that on AnyTree, whatever apps you distribute or use, are delivered exactly as they are supposed to be

AnyTree works with almost any package manager, so you can use it to deliver your apps exactly the same way you do today

GOSH has also collaborated with Ambassador Labs to assure the integrity of Docker Containers. The GOSH AnyTree Firewall for Telepresence adds an extra layer of security for Telepresence users by verifying the integrity of Docker containers as well as any changes made to them and builds Docker containers only from approved sources

AnyTree is currently available in beta on Linux, and will be coming soon to Mac and Windows. You can read more about it here

Or you can try it now: https://gosh.sh/anytree
7 June 2023

Hello everyone! BIG news for the entire TWA community.

We're finally sharing a design component library in Figma, which will make it easier for designers to design apps for TWA. The components fully mimic the Telegram interface, use it as a foundation, and inherit all existing principles.

Libraries are available for iOS and Android. Moreover, these same components are reused for designing the @wallet.

Please note that the libraries are in beta status, so bugs are possible.

Subscribe to the Figma community, click the 'Like' button! Don't forget to share feedback ‚Äì it will help with the release of new versions of the libraries.

Check this out!
